	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
	  var c = ca[i];

         <script>
          $(function () {
         function debounce(func, wait, immediate) {
            var timeout;
            return function() {
                var context = this, args = arguments;
                var later = function() {
                    timeout = null;
                    if (!immediate) func.apply(context, args);
                };
                var callNow = immediate && !timeout;
                clearTimeout(timeout);
                timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
                if (callNow) func.apply(context, args);
            };
        }
        $.fn.isInViewport = function() {
            var $element = $(this);
            var result = false;

            if ($element.length) {
                var $window = $(window);
                var elementTop = $element.offset().top;
                var viewportBottom = $window.scrollTop() + $window.height();

                result = elementTop < viewportBottom;
            }

            return result;
        };
        $(".js-lg-play-wrapper").on("click", function() {
            $(this).parent().find(".js-play-youtube").click();
            $(this).hide();
        });
        
        var $reveal = $(".js-lg-reveal");
        
        if (responsive.isMobile) {
            var $status = $('.pagingInfo');
            var $slickElement = $('.lg-content-carousel');

            $slickElement.on('init reInit afterChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide) {
                //currentSlide is undefined on init -- set it to 0 in this case (currentSlide is 0 based)
                var i = (currentSlide ? currentSlide : 0) + 1;
                $status.text(i + '/' + slick.slideCount);
            });
        } else if ($reveal.length) {
            $(window).on("load resize scroll", function() {
                debounce(function() {
                    $reveal.toggleClass("in-view", $reveal.isInViewport());
                }, 150, false)();
            });
        }
    });
         </script>

        <script>
         $(document).on('ready', function () {
        //resizeHeroSection();
        window.addEventListener('resize', resizeHeroSection, { passive: true });
        window.addEventListener('scroll', hideArrow, { passive: true });
        $('.js-header-slot-control').click(resizeHeroSection);
        resizeHeroSection();

        // Hero section wrapper class
        var imageWrapper = $('.js-page-height');
        var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
        var iOS = !!ua.match(/iP(ad|hone)/i) || !!ua.match(/iPhone/i);
        var webkit = !!ua.match(/WebKit/i);
        var iOSSafari = iOS && webkit && !ua.match(/CriOS/i);

        // move the arrow on ios safari due to the bottom nav bar overlapping it
        if (iOSSafari && window.innerWidth < 600) {
            $('.arrow-down').css('bottom', '50px')
        }

        // move the arrow on ios safari due to the bottom nav bar overlapping it
        if (iOSSafari && window.innerWidth < 325) {
            $('.arrow-down').css('bottom', '0px')
        }

        $('.js-hero-menu-item').hover(function () {
            var index = $('.js-hero-menu-item').index($(this));
            //$('.js-hero-img').eq(index).addClass('active');
        }, function () {
            //$('.js-hero-img').removeClass('active');
        });

        function resizeHeroSection() {
            if (window.innerHeight <= 420) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    //var heroHeight = $('.is-tab-mob').innerHeight() + 'px';
                    //console.log("here height is tiny.. mob landscape?" + window.innerHeight);
                    imageWrapper.css('height', '960px');
                }, 0);
            } else if (window.innerWidth >= 599 && window.innerWidth <= 951) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    //var heroHeight = $('.is-tab-mob').innerHeight() + 'px';
                    //console.log("here tab portrait");
                    imageWrapper.css('height', '460px');
                }, 0);
            } else {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    var headerHeight = window.responsive.isMobile ?
                        $('.js-site-header').innerHeight() + 'px' :
                        $('.header-main-content').innerHeight() + 'px';

                    var newHeight = 'calc(100vh - ' + headerHeight + ')';
                    imageWrapper.css('height', newHeight);
                }, 500);
            }
        }

        function hideArrow() {
            if (window.innerWidth >= 599 && window.innerWidth <= 951) {
                return false;
            }

            var arrow = $('.arrow-down');
            var initialOffset = $('.js-hero-wrapper').offset().top;
            var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
            var curentOffset = scrollTop - initialOffset;
            var hideThreshold = window.responsive.isMobile ? 60 : 180;

            if (curentOffset > hideThreshold) {
                arrow.fadeOut();
            } else {
                arrow.fadeIn();
            }
        }
    });
        </script>

        <script>
         $(function () {
        $('.js-video-placeholder').on('click', function () {
            $(this).hide();
            YT.get('offWhiteVid').playVideo()
        });

        // hero switch image and cta
        var active_menu_item = 0;
        $('.js-hero-menu-item').hover(function () {
            var link_position = $('.js-hero-menu-item').index($(this));
            //the corresponding img to the link number
            var $correspondingImg = $('.js-hero-img').eq(link_position);

            window.clearInterval(bg_change); //stops the loop on hover

            //this is all on hover, so now add the active class
            $('.js-hero-img').removeClass('active');  //removing the timed hover class  - to stop a double active remove from all
            $('.js-hero-menu-item').removeClass('js-bg'); // to stop the extra loop?
            $correspondingImg.addClass('active');
            $('.js-img-holder').addClass('active-overlay');
            $('.js-hero-wrapper').addClass('overlay-active');
        }, function () {
            $('.js-img-holder').removeClass('active-overlay');
            $('.js-hero-wrapper').removeClass('overlay-active');
            active_menu_item = $('.js-hero-menu-item').index($(this));
            //console.log("after hover: " + active_menu_item);
            bg_change = setInterval(switchBG, 3500); // restarts the loop
        });

        var switchBG = function () {
            var menu_items = $('.js-hero-menu-item').length;
            //var active_menu_item = 0;
            if ($('.js-hero-menu-item.js-bg').index() == menu_items - 1) {
                active_menu_item = 0;
                //console.log("after menu_items-1: " + active_menu_item);
            } else if (active_menu_item == menu_items - 1) {
                active_menu_item = 0;
                //console.log("uahfh"  + active_menu_item);
            } else {
                active_menu_item++;
                //console.log("after ++: " + active_menu_item);
            }
            $('.js-hero-menu-item.js-bg').removeClass('js-bg');
            $('.js-hero-img').removeClass('active');
            $('.js-hero-menu-item').eq(active_menu_item).addClass('js-bg');
            $('.js-hero-img').eq(active_menu_item).addClass('active');
        }
        // if (!window.responsive.isMobile){
        var bg_change = setInterval(switchBG, 3500);  //this one starts on page load, image change
        //console.log('start');
        // }
        // Select all links with hashes
        $('a[href*="#"]')
            // Remove links that don't actually link to anything
            .not('[href="#"]')
            .not('[href="#0"]')
            .click(function (event) {
                // On-page links
                if (
                    location.pathname.replace(/^\//, '') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//, '')
                    &&
                    location.hostname == this.hostname
                ) {
                    // Figure out element to scroll to
                    var target = $(this.hash);
                    target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) + ']');
                    // Does a scroll target exist?
                    if (target.length) {
                        // Only prevent default if animation is actually gonna happen
                        event.preventDefault();
                        $('html, body').animate({
                            scrollTop: target.offset().top
                        }, 1000, function () {
                            // Callback after animation
                            // Must change focus!
                            var $target = $(target);
                            $target.focus();
                            if ($target.is(":focus")) { // Checking if the target was focused
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                $target.attr('tabindex', '-1'); // Adding tabindex for elements not focusable
                                $target.focus(); // Set focus again
                            };
                        });
                    }
                }
            });

    });
        </script>

          <script>
           $(function() {
		var fakeInput = '<span class="fake-checkbox"></span>';
		var requiredIndicator = '<span class="f-required-marker"><span aria-hidden="true">* </span><span class="visuallyhidden">Required field</span></span>';

		removeAgesTooYoung();
		updateOptInPrivacyPolicyText('Ich habe die <a href="https://row.jimmychoo.com/de_DE/kundenservice/privacy-policy.html" class="js-privacy-policy">Datenschutzrichtiline</a> gelesen und verstanden und akzeptiere die Verarbeitung meiner personenbezogenen Daten durch Jimmy Choo.')

		if (window.pageContext.type === 'orderconfirmation' || window.pageContext.checkoutStep === 'billing') {
			updateNewsletterConsentText('Ich möchte über Produkte, Dienstleistungen, Events, Handels-und Marketing-Aktionen der Jimmy Choo Gruppe (einschließlich personalisiertem Online-Inhalt und Werbung durch die Jimmy Choo Websites, sozialen Netzwerke oder unseren Online-Partnern) informiert werden. Weitere Informationen befinden sich in Jimmy Choo’s <a href="https://row.jimmychoo.com/de_DE/kundenservice/privacy-policy.html" class="js-privacy-policy">Datenschutzrichtiline</a>.');
		} else {
			updateNewsletterConsentText('Durch die Registrierung akzeptieren Sie, Informationen von der Jimmy Choo Gruppe über Produkte, Dienstleistungen, Events, Handels-und Marketing-Aktionen (einschließlich personalisierten Online-Inhalt und Werbung durch die Jimmy Choo Websites, sozialen Netzwerke oder unsere Online-Partner) zu erhalten. Für weitere Informationen lesen Sie bitte unsere <a href="https://row.jimmychoo.com/de_DE/kundenservice/privacy-policy.html" class="js-privacy-policy">Datenschutzrichtiline</a>.');
		}


		/**
		 * Get the HTML of the input field inside of `$wrapper`.
		 * This allows reuse of code for differently named input fields.
		 */
		function getInputHTML($wrapper) {
			var $input = $wrapper.find('input');

			if (!$input.length) return '';

			return $input[0].outerHTML;
		}

		/**
		 * BAU-4812 - Account Registration - News Letter Marketing Consent Text Update | C2 Label
		 * BAU-4864 - Account Details - Opt in Privacy Policy Text | C2 Label
		 *
		 */
		function updateNewsletterConsentText(text) {
			var $label = $('.js-addtoemaillist .f-label');

			$label.html(getInputHTML($label) + fakeInput + text);
		}

		/**
		 * BAU-4813 - Account Registration - Opt in Privacy Policy Text | C9 Label
		 * BAU-4852 - Account Details - Opt in Privacy Policy Text | C9 Label
		 * BAU-4834 - Post Checkout Registration | C5 Label
		 */
		function updateOptInPrivacyPolicyText(text) {
			var $label = $('.terms-conditions-label');

			$label.html(getInputHTML($label) + fakeInput + requiredIndicator + text);
		}

		/**
		 * BAU-4817 - My Account Registration - Removing Years Values via the DOB field
		 */
		function removeAgesTooYoung() {
			$('.js-birthday-year .f-select_option').each(function(){
				if(parseInt(this.value) > 2002) {
					$(this).remove();
				}
			});
		}
	});
          </script>
